## Definitions

### Commuting squares of maps induce commuting squares of precomposition maps

Every commuting square

```text
            top
       A --------> X
       |           |
  left |           | right
       ∨           ∨
       B --------> Y
          bottom
```

induces a commuting square of
[precomposition functions](foundation-core.precomposition-functions.md)

```text
                         precomp right S
                (A → S) -----------------> (X → S)
                   |                           |
  precomp bottom S |                           | precomp top S
                   ∨                           ∨
                (B → S) ------------------> (Y → S).
                          precomp left S
```

### Commuting squares of maps induce commuting squares of postcomposition maps

Every commuting square

```text
            top
       A --------> X
       |           |
  left |           | right
       ∨           ∨
       B --------> Y
          bottom
```

induces a commuting square of
[postcomposition functions](foundation-core.postcomposition-functions.md)

```text
                        postcomp S top
              (S → A) ------------------> (S → X)
                 |                           |
 postcomp S left |                           | postcomp S right
                 ∨                           ∨
              (S → B) ------------------> (S → Y).
                       postcomp S bottom
```

## Properties

### Taking vertical inversions of squares is an inverse operation

Vertical composition of a square with the square obtained by inverting the
vertical maps fits into a [prism](foundation.commuting-prisms-of-maps.md) with
the reflexivity square.

The analogous result for horizontal composition remains to be formalized.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="4549" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="4556" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#4556" class="Module">_</a>

### Associativity of vertical pasting

The proof of associativity of horizontal pasting may be found in
[`foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps`](foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.md).

      <a id="12618" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12620" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10879" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="12633" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="12636" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12637" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10989" class="Bound">sq-mid</a> <a id="12644" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="12647" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10734" class="Bound">top-left</a><a id="12655" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="12664" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12666" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="12668" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10879" class="Bound">bottom-right</a> <a id="12681" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="12683" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10813" class="Bound">mid-right</a><a id="12692" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12694" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="12697" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#10922" class="Bound">sq-top</a><a id="12703" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Naturality of commuting squares of maps with respect to identifications

Similarly to the naturality square of homotopies and
[identifications](foundation-core.identity-types.md), we have a naturality
square of coherence squares of maps and identifications:

```text
            ap f (ap g p)
   f (g x) ---------------> f (g y)
      |                       |
  H x |                       | H y
      ∨                       ∨
   h (k x) ---------------> h (k y)
            ap h (ap k p)           .
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="13231" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="13238" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13238" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="13242" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="13244" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13244" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="13247" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13247" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="13250" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13250" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="13253" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13253" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="13256" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13258" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="13263" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13265" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13266" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13266" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13268" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13270" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="13273" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13244" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="13275" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13277" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13278" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13278" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13280" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13282" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="13285" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13247" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="13287" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13289" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13290" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13290" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13292" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13294" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="13297" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13250" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="13299" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13301" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="13302" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13302" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="13304" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13306" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="13309" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13253" class="Bound">l4</a><a id="13311" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="13315" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13317" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13317" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="13321" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13323" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13266" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13325" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13327" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13278" class="Bound">B</a><a id="13328" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13330" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13331" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13331" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="13336" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13338" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13266" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="13340" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13342" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13290" class="Bound">C</a><a id="13343" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13345" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13346" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13346" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="13352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13354" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13278" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="13356" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13358" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13302" class="Bound">D</a><a id="13359" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13361" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13362" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13362" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="13369" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13371" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13290" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="13373" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="13375" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13302" class="Bound">D</a><a id="13376" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13380" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13382" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13382" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13384" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13386" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#1303" class="Function">coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="13408" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13317" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="13412" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13331" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="13417" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13346" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="13423" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13362" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="13429" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13433" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="13442" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13442" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="13468" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="13474" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="13476" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13476" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13478" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13478" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="13480" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13482" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13266" class="Bound">A</a><a id="13483" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="13485" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13486" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13486" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="13488" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13490" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13476" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="13492" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2713" class="Function Operator">＝</a> <a id="13494" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13478" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13495" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="13497" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="13503" href="foundation-core.commuting-squares-of-identifications.html#1275" class="Function">coherence-square-identifications</a>
      <a id="13542" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13544" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13547" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13362" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="13554" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13555" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13558" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13331" class="Bound">left</a> <a id="13563" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13486" class="Bound">p</a><a id="13564" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="13573" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13575" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13382" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13577" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13476" class="Bound">x</a><a id="13578" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13586" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13588" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13382" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="13590" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13478" class="Bound">y</a><a id="13591" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="13599" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="13601" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13604" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13346" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="13610" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13611" href="foundation.action-on-identifications-functions.html#730" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="13614" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13317" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="13618" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13486" class="Bound">p</a><a id="13619" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="13624" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13442" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="13650" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2682" class="InductiveConstructor">refl</a> <a id="13655" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13657" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#8258" class="Function">right-unit</a>
</pre>
As a corollary, whenever we have two coherence squares touching at a vertex:

```text
  A -----> B
  |        |
  |   H ⇗  |
  ∨        ∨
  C -----> D -----> X
           |        |
           |   K ⇗  |
           ∨        ∨
           Y -----> Z ,
```

there is a homotopy between first applying `H`, then `K`, and first applying
`K`, then `H`.

      <a id="14578" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14580" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14369" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="14582" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="14585" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14195" class="Bound">mid-top</a> <a id="14593" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="14596" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14166" class="Bound">top</a><a id="14599" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="14607" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14609" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14276" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="14615" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="14618" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14235" class="Bound">mid-right</a> <a id="14628" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="14631" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14312" class="Bound">H</a><a id="14632" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="14636" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14441" class="Function">swap-nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="14667" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14667" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="14669" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="14675" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#13442" class="Function">nat-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="14701" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14235" class="Bound">mid-right</a> <a id="14711" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14255" class="Bound">mid-bottom</a> <a id="14722" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14276" class="Bound">right</a> <a id="14728" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14292" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="14735" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14369" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="14737" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14738" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14312" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="14740" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#14667" class="Bound">x</a><a id="14741" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### Commutativity of horizontal and vertical pasting

Given a square of commuting squares, like so:

```text
  A -----> B -----> C
  |        |        |
  |    ⇗   |    ⇗   |
  ∨        ∨        ∨
  X -----> Y -----> Z
  |        |        |
  |    ⇗   |    ⇗   |
  ∨        ∨        ∨
  M -----> N -----> O ,
```

we have two choices for obtaining the outer commuting square — either by first
vertically composing the smaller squares, and then horizontally composing the
newly created rectangles, or by first horizontally composing the squares, and
then vertically composing the rectangles.

The following lemma states that the big squares obtained by these two
compositions are again homotopic. Diagrammatically, we have

```text
 H | K   H | K
 ----- ~ --|--
 L | T   L | T .
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="15539" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="15546" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#15546" class="Module">_</a>

</pre>
### Distributivity of pasting squares and transposing by precomposition

Given two commuting squares which can be composed horizontally (vertically), we
know that composing them and then transposing them by precomposition gives a
homotopy that is homotopic to first transposing the squares and then composing
them.

```text
          tl       tr                tr ∘ tl
      A -----> B -----> C         A --------> C
      |        |        |         |           |
    l |   H  m |   K    | r  ↦  l |   H | K   | r
      ∨        ∨        ∨         ∨           ∨
      X -----> Y -----> Z         X --------> Z
          bl       br                br ∘ bl

               ↧                        ↧

             - ∘ r
        W^Z ------> W^C
         |           |
  - ∘ br |    W^K    | - ∘ tr        W^(H | K)
         ∨   - ∘ m   ∨                  ~
        W^Y ------> W^B       ↦
         |           |                 W^K
  - ∘ bl |    W^H    | - ∘ tl          ---
         ∨           ∨                 W^H
        W^X ------> W^A
             - ∘ l
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="20057" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="20064" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#20064" class="Module">_</a>

      <a id="24386" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#14276" class="Function">＝</a> <a id="24388" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#3905" class="Postulate">eq-htpy</a>
          <a id="24406" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24408" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24409" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24411" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24414" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23993" class="Bound">K</a><a id="24415" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24417" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="24420" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23884" class="Bound">left-top</a><a id="24428" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24430" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#5864" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="24440" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#3905" class="Postulate">eq-htpy</a>
          <a id="24458" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24460" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24462" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24465" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24466" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23950" class="Bound">right-bottom</a> <a id="24479" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24482" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23984" class="Bound">H</a><a id="24483" class="Symbol">))</a>
        <a id="24494" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#14276" class="Function">by</a>
        <a id="24505" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#6345" class="Function">eq-htpy-concat-htpy</a>
          <a id="24535" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24538" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24540" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24543" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23993" class="Bound">K</a><a id="24544" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24546" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2725" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="24549" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23884" class="Bound">left-top</a><a id="24557" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="24618" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24620" href="foundation-core.precomposition-functions.html#582" class="Function">precomp</a> <a id="24628" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23884" class="Bound">left-top</a> <a id="24637" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#20179" class="Bound">W</a><a id="24638" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="24650" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24652" href="foundation.precomposition-functions.html#1431" class="Function">htpy-precomp</a> <a id="24665" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23993" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="24667" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#20179" class="Bound">W</a> <a id="24669" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a><a id="24670" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24672" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#5864" class="Function Operator">∙</a>
        <a id="24682" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#3905" class="Postulate">eq-htpy</a>
          <a id="24700" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24702" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24703" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24705" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="24707" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23950" class="Bound">right-bottom</a><a id="24719" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24721" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24724" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23984" class="Bound">H</a><a id="24725" class="Symbol">)</a>

          <a id="24766" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24768" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="24770" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24770" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="24772" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24772" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="24774" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="24776" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24770" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="24778" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#5864" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="24780" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#3905" class="Postulate">eq-htpy</a> <a id="24788" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24772" class="Bound">L</a><a id="24789" class="Symbol">)</a>
          <a id="24801" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24803" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#6168" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="24807" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24808" href="foundation.precomposition-functions.html#6054" class="Function">compute-eq-htpy-ap-precomp</a> <a id="24835" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23884" class="Bound">left-top</a> <a id="24844" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24845" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24847" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="24850" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23993" class="Bound">K</a><a id="24851" class="Symbol">)))</a>
          <a id="24865" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="24867" href="foundation.function-extensionality.html#3905" class="Postulate">eq-htpy</a> <a id="24875" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24876" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#7848" class="Function">preserves-comp-left-whisker-comp</a> <a id="24909" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#24002" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="24911" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23950" class="Bound">right-bottom</a> <a id="24924" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#23984" class="Bound">H</a><a id="24925" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### Transposing by precomposition of whiskered squares

Taking a square of the form

```text
      f        top
  X -----> A -----> B
           |        |
      left |   H    | right
           ∨        ∨
           C -----> D
             bottom
```

and transposing it by precomposition results in the square

```text
  W^D -----> W^B
   |          |
   |   W^H    |
   ∨          ∨  - ∘ f
  W^C -----> W^A -----> W^X
```

This fact can be written as distribution of right whiskering over transposition:
`W^(H ·r f) = W^f ·l W^H`.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="25476" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="25483" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25483" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="25487" class="Symbol">{</a> <a id="25489" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25489" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="25492" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25492" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="25495" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25495" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="25498" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25498" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="25501" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25501" class="Bound">l5</a> <a id="25504" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25504" class="Bound">l6</a> <a id="25507" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25509" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="25514" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="25711" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="25720" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25720" class="Function">distributive-precomp-right-whisker-comp-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="25782" class="Symbol">:</a>

      <a id="25925" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="25927" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25580" class="Bound">W</a><a id="25928" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25930" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a>

  <a id="26024" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25720" class="Function">distributive-precomp-right-whisker-comp-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="26086" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26086" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26088" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26088" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="26090" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="26096" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#6168" class="Function">inv</a> <a id="26100" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26101" href="foundation.precomposition-functions.html#6054" class="Function">compute-eq-htpy-ap-precomp</a> <a id="26128" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26086" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26130" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="26131" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26088" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="26133" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="26136" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25660" class="Bound">H</a><a id="26137" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
Similarly, we can calculate transpositions of left-whiskered squares with the
formula `W^(f ·l H) = W^H ·r W^f`.

<pre class="Agda">  <a id="26269" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26269" class="Function">distributive-precomp-left-whisker-comp-coherence-square-maps</a> <a id="26330" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="26336" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26338" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26338" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26340" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="26342" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25556" class="Bound">D</a> <a id="26344" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="26346" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25568" class="Bound">X</a><a id="26347" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26349" class="Symbol">→</a>
    <a id="26355" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#2188" class="Function">precomp-coherence-square-maps</a>
      <a id="26391" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26393" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25595" class="Bound">top</a><a id="26396" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26404" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26406" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25609" class="Bound">left</a><a id="26410" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26418" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26420" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26338" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26422" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="26424" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25624" class="Bound">right</a><a id="26429" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26437" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26439" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26338" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26441" href="foundation-core.function-types.html#455" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="26443" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25640" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="26449" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26457" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26459" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26338" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="26461" href="foundation.whiskering-homotopies-composition.html#2364" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="26464" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25660" class="Bound">H</a><a id="26465" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="26473" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="26475" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#25580" class="Bound">W</a><a id="26476" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="26478" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2535" class="Function Operator">~</a>

</pre>
### The square of function spaces induced by a composition of triangles is homotopic to the composition of induced triangles of function spaces

    <a id="30438" href="foundation.precomposition-functions.html#1884" class="Function">compute-concat-htpy-precomp</a> <a id="30466" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#30411" class="Bound">H</a> <a id="30468" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#30420" class="Bound">K</a> <a id="30470" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#26943" class="Bound">W</a> <a id="30472" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#30429" class="Bound">h</a>
</pre>
### Collapsing inner squares in pasted squares composed of triangles

Consider two commuting squares, composed in total of four commuting triangles,
which take the following form:

```text
           top
     A -----------> C
     |             ∧|
     |           /  |
     |     bl  /    |
  tl |       /      | tr
     |     /        |
     |   /          |
     ∨ /    mid     ∨
     B -----------> Y
     |             ∧|
     |           /  |
     |     tr  /    |
  bl |       /      | br
     |     /        |
     |   /          |
     ∨ /            ∨
     C -----------> Z .
          bottom
```

Note that the bottom-left vertex is the same as the top-right vertex, and the
diagonals are not arbitrary.

If the square that arises in the middle,

```text
        bl
     B ----> C
     |       |
  bl |       | tr
     ∨       ∨
     C ----> Y ,
        tr
```

is homotopic to the reflexive homotopy `refl-htpy : tr ∘ bl ~ tr ∘ bl`, then the
whole rectangle collapses (is homotopic) to the
[horizontal composition](foundation.homotopy-algebra.md)

```text
                         Y
                        ∧ \
                  tr  /     \  br
                    /         \
        top       /             ∨
  A -----------> C -----------> Z .
   \             ∧    bottom
     \         /
   tl  \     /  bl
         ∨ /
          B
```

<pre class="Agda"><a id="31841" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="31848" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31848" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="31852" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31853" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31853" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="31856" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31856" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="31859" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31859" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="31862" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31862" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="31865" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31865" class="Bound">l5</a> <a id="31868" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31870" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="31875" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="31879" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31880" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31880" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="31882" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31884" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="31887" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31853" class="Bound">l1</a><a id="31889" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31891" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31892" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31892" class="Bound">B</a> <a id="31894" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31896" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="31899" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31856" class="Bound">l2</a><a id="31901" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="31903" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="31904" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31904" class="Bound">C</a> <a id="31906" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="31908" href="Agda.Primitive.html#388" class="Primitive">UU</a> <a id="31911" href="foundation.commuting-squares-of-maps.html#31859" class="Bound">l3</a><a id="31913" class="Symbol">}</a>

    <a id="34121" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="34123" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#8353" class="Function">ap-concat-htpy&#39;</a>
